1 manag wesan the he his mod spanan 
2 that he word god wisian biginnan 
3 rekkian the giruni that the riki Krist 
4 undar mankunni maritha frummian 
5 mid word endi mid werk the willian tho wis filo 
6 liudi barn lovon lera Krist 
7 helag word god endi mid iru hand skrivan 
8 berhtliko an bok hwo he is gibodskepi skulan 
9 frummian firihos barn than wesan thoh he fiuwar te the 
10 undar the menigi the hebbian maht god 
11 helpa fan himil helag gest 
12 kraft fan Krist he werthan kiosan te the 
13 that he the evangelium en skulan 
14 an bok skrivan endi so manag gibod god 
15 helag himilisk word he ne motan helith than mer 
16 firihos barn frummian newan that he fiuwar te the 
17 thurh kraft god kiosan werthan 
18 Matheus endi Matheus so wesan the man hetan 
19 Lukas endi Johannes he wesan god liof 
20 wirthig te the giwerki hebbian he waldand god 
21 the helith an iru herta helag gest 
22 fasto bifelhan endi feraht hugi 
23 so manag wislik word endi giwit mikil 
24 that he skulan ahebbian helag stemna 
25 godspel the god the ne hebbian enig gigado hwergin 
26 the word an these werold the eo waldand mer 
27 drohtin diurian eftha dervi thing 
28 firinwerk fellian eftha fiund nith 
29 strid witharstandan hwand he hebbian stark hugi 
30 mildi endi god the the mester wesan 
31 athalordfrumo alomahtig 
32 the skulan he fiuwar tho fingar skrivan 
33 settian endi singan endi seggian forth 
34 the he fan Krist kraft the mikil 
35 sehan endi horian the he self sprekan 
36 wisian endi wirkian wundarlik filo 
37 so manag mid man mahtig drohtin 
38 al so he it fan the anagin thurh is en kraft 
39 waldand sprekan tho he erist these werold skeppian 
40 endi tho al bifahan mid en word 
41 himil endi ertha endi al the he bihlidan egan 
42 wirkian endi wahsan the werthan tho al mid word god 
43 fasto bifahan endi frummian aftar the 
44 hwilik than liudskepi land skulan 
45 wido waldan eftha hwar the werold skulan 
46 aldar endion en wesan he tho noh than 
47 firihos barn biforan endi the fif wesan agangan 
48 skulan tho the sehsto saliglik 
49 kuman thurh kraft god endi Krist giburd 
50 helian bet helag gest 
51 an these middilgard manag te helpa 
52 firihos barn te fruma with fiund nith 
53 with derni dwalm than hebbian tho drohtin god 
54 Roman liudi farlihan riki mer 
55 hebbian the heriskepi herta sterkian 
56 that he hebbian bithwingan thiod gihwilik 
57 hebbian fan Rumuburg riki winnan 
58 helmgitrostio sittian iru heritogo 
59 an land gihwe hebbian liudi giwald 
60 al elithioda Erodes wesan 
61 an Hierusalem ovar the Judeo folk 
62 kiosan te kuning so he the kesur tharod 
63 fan Rumuburg riki thiodan 
64 settian undar the gisithi he ne wesan thoh mid sibbia bilang 
65 avaro Israhel ethiligiburd 
66 kuman fan iru knosal newan that he thurh the kesur thank 
67 fan Rumuburg riki hebbian 
68 that he wesan so gihorig hildiskalk 
69 avaro Israhel ellianrof 
70 switho unwand wini than lang he giwald egan 
71 Erodes the riki endi radburd haldan 
72 Judeo liudi than wesan thar en gamalon man 
73 the wesan frod gumo hebbian feraht hugi 
74 wesan fan the liudi Levi kunni 
75 Jakob sunu god thiod 
76 Zacharias wesan he hetan the wesan so salig man 
77 hwand he simblon gern god thionon 
78 wirkian aftar is willio don is wif so self 
79 wesan siu aldron idis ne motan he erviward 
80 an iru juguthhed gividig werthan 
81 libbian he farutar lastar wirkian lof god 
82 wesan so gihorig hevankuning 
83 diurian usa drohtin ne willian dervi wiht 
84 undar mankunni men frummian 
85 saka sundia wesan he thoh an sorga hugi 
86 that he erviward egan ne motan 
87 ak wesan he barn los than skulan he gibod god 
88 thar an Hierusalem so oft so gigengi standan 
89 that he torhtliko tid manon 
90 so skulan he at the wih waldand geld 
91 helag bihwervan hevankuning 
92 god jungarskepi gern wesan he switho 
93 that he it thurh feraht hugi fremmian motan 
94 tho werthan the tid kuman the thar tellian hebbian 
95 wis man mid word that skulan the wih god 
96 Zacharias bisehan tho werthan thar samnon filo 
97 thar te Hierusalem Judeo liudi 
98 werod te the wih thar he waldand god 
99 switho thioliko thiggian skulan 
100 herro is huldi that he hevankuning 
101 leth alatan the liudi standan 
102 umbi the helag hus endi gangan he the heron man 
103 an the wih innan the werod othar bidan 
104 umbi the alah utan Ebreo liudi 
105 hwan er the frod man frummian hebbian 
106 waldand willio so he tho the wihrok dragan 
107 ald aftar the alah endi umbi the altari gangan 
108 mid is rokfat riki thionon 
109 frummian ferahtliko fraho sin 
110 god jungarskepi gern switho 
111 mid hluttar hugi so man herro skulan 
112 gern fulgangan gruri kuman he 
113 egiso an the alah he sehan thar aftar the en engil god 
114 an the wih innan he sprekan he mid is word to 
115 hetan that frod gumo forht ne wesan 
116 hetan that he he ne andradan thin dad wesan kwethan he 
117 waldand werth endi thin word so self 
118 thin thionost wesan he an thank that thu sulik githaht hebbian 
119 an he en kraft ik is engil wesan 
120 Gabriel wesan ik hetan the eo for god standan 
121 andward for the alowaldo ne wesan that he ik an is arundi hwarod 
122 sendian willian nu hetan he ik an these sith faran 
123 hetan that ik thu thoh kuthian that thu kind beran 
124 fan thin ald idis odan skulan 
125 werthan an these werold word spah 
126 the ne skulan an is lif eo lith andbitan 
127 win an is werold so hebbian he wurdigiskap 
128 metod markon endi maht god 
129 hetan that ik thu thoh seggian that it skulan gisith wesan 
130 hevankuning hetan that gi it haldan wel 
131 tiohan thurh treuwa kwethan that he he tir so filo 
132 an god riki fargevan willian 
133 he kwethan that the god gumo Johannes te namo 
134 hebbian skulan biodan that gi it hetan so 
135 the kind than it kuman kwethan that it Krist gisith 
136 an these wid werold werthan skulan 
137 he self sunu endi kwethan that he sniumo herod 
138 an is gibodskepi bethia kuman 
139 Zacharias tho mahlian endi with self sprekan 
140 drohtin engil endi he the dad biginnan 
141 wundron the word hwo mugan the werthan so kwethan he 
142 aftar an aldar it wesan wit al te lat 
143 so te winnan so thu mid thin word sprekan 
144 hwand wit hebbian aldar er efno twentig 
145 wintar an unka werold er than kuman the wif te ik 
146 than wesan wit nu atsamne antsivunta wintar 
147 gibenkio endi gibeddio sithor ik siu ik te brud kiosan 
148 so wit the an unka juguth girnian ne mugan 
149 that wit erviward egan motan 
150 fodian an unka fletti nu wit sus frodon wesan 
151 hebbian wit eldi biniman elliandad 
152 that wit wesan an unka siun slekkian endi an unka sida lat 
153 flesk wesan wit afallan fel unskoni 
154 wesan unka lud lithan lik drusinon 
155 wesan unka andbari otharlik 
156 mod endi meginkraft so wit ju so manag dag 
157 wesan an these werold so ik the wundar thunkian 
158 hwe it so werthan mugan so thu mid thin word sprekan 
159 tho werthan the hevankuning bodo harm an is mod 
160 that he is giwerk so wundron skulan 
161 endi the ne willian huggian that he mugan helag god 
162 so alajung so he fan erist wesan 
163 self wirkian ef he so willian 
164 skerian he tho te witan that he ne mugan enig word sprekan 
165 mahlian mid is muth er than thu magu werthan 
166 fan thin ald idis erl afodian 
167 kindjung beran kunni god 
168 wanam te these werold than skulan thu eft sprekan 
169 hebbian thin stemna giwald ne thurvan thu stum wesan 
170 lang hwila tho werthan it san lestian so 
171 werthan te war so thar an the wih sprekan 
172 engil the alowaldo werthan ald gumo 
173 spraka bilosian thoh he spah hugi 
174 beran an is briost bidan al dag 
175 the werod for the wih endi wundron al 
176 bihwi he thar so lango lofsalig man 
177 switho frod gumo fraho sin 
178 thionon thurvan so thar er enig thegan ne don 
179 than he thar an the wih waldand geld 
180 folm frummian tho kuman frod gumo 
181 ut fan the alah erl thringan 
182 nah mikil wesan he niud mikil 
183 hwe he he sothlik seggian willian 
184 wisian te war he ne mugan tho enig word sprekan 
185 seggian the gisithi newan that he mid is swith hand 
186 wisian the werod that he usa waldand 
187 lera lestian the liudi farstandan 
188 that he thar hebbian gegnungo godkund hwe 
189 farsehan self thoh he it ne mugan seggian wiht 
190 wisian te war tho hebbian he usa waldand 
191 geld lestian al so is gigengi wesan 
192 markon mid man tho werthan san aftar the maht god 
193 kuthian is kraft mikil werthan the kwen okan 
194 idis an iru eldi skulan he erviward 
195 switho godkund gumo gividig werthan 
196 barn an burg bidan aftar the 
197 the wif wurdigiskap skridan the wintar forth 
198 gangan the ger gital Johannes kuman 
199 an liudi lioht lik wesan he skoni 
200 wesan he fel fagar fahs endi nagal 
201 wanga wesan he wlitig tho faran thar wis man 
202 snel tesamna the swas mer 
203 wundron the giwerki bihwi it eo mugan werthan so 
204 that undar so ald twene odan werthan 
205 barn an giburd ne wesan that it gibod god 
206 self wesan ansebbian he garo 
207 that it elkor so wanlik werthan ne mugan 
208 tho sprekan thar en frodon man the so filo kunnan 
209 wis word hebbian giwit mikil 
210 fragon niudliko hwe is namo skulan 
211 wesan an these werold ik thunkian an is wisa giliko 
212 jak an is gibari that he wesan bet than we 
213 so ik wanian that he we gegnungo god fan himil 
214 self sendian tho sprekan san aftar the 
215 modar the kind the the magu hebbian 
216 the barn an iru barm her kuman gibod god kwethan siu 
217 fern ger formo word 
218 biodan that he Johannes bi god lera 
219 hetan skulan the ik an min hugi ne durran 
220 wendian mid wiht ef ik it waldan motan 
221 tho sprekan en gelhert man the iru gaduling wesan 
222 ne hetan er eowiht so kwethan he athalboran 
223 usa kunni eftha knosal wita kiosan he othar 
224 niudsam namo he niotan ef he motan 
225 tho sprekan eft the frod man the thar kunnan filo mahlian 
226 ne gevan ik the te rad kwethan he rink 
227 that he word god wendian biginnan 
228 ak wita it the fadar fragon the thar so frodon sittian 
229 wis an is winseli thoh he ne mugan enig word sprekan 
230 thoh mugan he bi bokstaf bref wirkian 
231 namo skrivan tho he nah gangan 
232 leggian he en bok an barm endi biddian gern 
233 writan wisliko wordgimerki 
234 hwe he the helag barn hetan skulan 
235 tho niman he the bok an hand endi an is hugi thenkian 
236 switho gern te god Johannes namo 
237 wisliko writan endi ok aftar mid is word sprekan 
238 switho spahliko hebbian he eft is spraka giwald 
239 giwit endi wisa the witi wesan tho agangan 
240 hard harmskara the he helag god 
241 mahtig makon that he an is modsevo 
242 god ne fargetan than he he eft sendian is jungaro to 
243 tho ne wesan lang aftar the it al so lestian werthan 
244 so he mankunni manag hwila 
245 god alomahtig fargevan hebbian 
246 that he is himilisk barn herod te werold 
247 he self sunu sendian willian 
248 te the that he her alosian al liudstamn 
249 werod fan witan werthan is wisbodo 
250 an Galilealand Gabriel kuman 
251 engil the alowaldo thar he en idis witan 
252 munilik magath Maria wesan siu hetan 
253 wesan siu thiorna thihan siu en thegan hebbian 
254 Joseph mahlian god kunni man 
255 the David dohtar the wesan so diurlik wif 
256 idis andheti thar siu the engil god 
257 an Nazarethburg bi namo self 
258 grotian geginward endi siu fan god kweddian 
259 hel wesan thu Maria kwethan he thu wesan thin herro liof 
260 waldand wirthig hwand thu giwit hebbian 
261 idis anst ful thu skulan furi al wesan 
262 wif wihian ne hebbian thu wek hugi 
263 ne forhtian thu thin ferah ne kuman ik thu te enig fresa herod 
264 ne dragan ik enig drugi thing thu skulan usa drohtin wesan 
265 modar mid man endi skulan the magu fodian 
266 the hoh himilkuning sunu the skulan helian te namo 
267 egan mid eldi endi ne kuman 
268 the wid riki giwand the he waldan skulan 
269 mari thiodan tho sprekan he eft the magath angegin 
270 with the engil god idis skoni 
271 al wif wlitig hwo mugan the werthan so kwethan siu 
272 that ik magu fodian ik eo man ne werthan 
273 wis an min werold tho hebbian eft is word garu 
274 engil the alowaldo the idis tegegnes 
275 an thu skulan helag gest fan hevanwang 
276 kuman thurh kraft god thanan skulan thu kind odan 
277 werthan an these werold waldand kraft 
278 skulan thu fan the hoh hevankuning 
279 skadoian mid skimo ne werthan skoni giburd 
280 so mari mid man hwand siu kuman thurh maht god 
281 an these wid werold tho werthan the wif hugi 
282 aftar the arundi al hwervan 
283 an god willio than ik her garu standan kwethan siu 
284 te sulik ambahtskepi so he ik egan willian 
285 thiu wesan ik thiodgod nu ik the thing truon 
286 werthan ik aftar thin word al so he willio wesan 
287 herro min ik hugi twifli 
288 word wisa so fregnan ik that the wif andfahan 
289 the god arundi gern switho 
290 mid lioht hugi endi mid gilovo god 
291 endi mid hluttar treuwa werthan tho the helag gest 
292 the barn an iru bosom endi siu an iru briost farstandan 
293 jak an iru sevo self seggian the siu willian 
294 that siu hebbian okan the alowaldo kraft 
295 helag fan himil tho werthan hugi Joseph 
296 is mod worrian the he er the magath hebbian 
297 the idis andheti athaliknosal wif 
298 buggian he te brud he afsebbian the that siu hebbian barn undar siu 
299 ne wanian the mid wiht newa that siu the wif hebbian 
300 wardon so warliko ne witan he waldand tho noh 
301 blithi gibodskepi ne willian siu he te brud tho 
302 halon he te hiwa ak biginnan he tho an is hugi thenkian 
303 hwo he siu tho farlatan so siu thar ne werthan leth wiht 
304 odan arved ne willian siu aftar the 
305 meldon for menigi andradan that siu man barn 
306 lif biniman so wesan than the liudi thau 
307 thurh the ald eo Ebreo folk 
308 so hwilik so thar an unreht idis hiwian 
309 that siu simbla the bedskepi buggian skulan 
310 fri mid iru ferah ne wesan eo the femia so god 
311 that siu eo mid the liudi lango libbian motan 
312 wesan undar the werod tho biginnan he the wis man 
313 switho god gumo Joseph an is mod 
314 thenkian the thing hwo he the thiorna tho 
315 list farlatan tho ne wesan lang te the 
316 that he thar an drom kuman drohtin engil 
317 hevankuning bodo endi hetan siu he haldan wel 
318 minnion siu an is mod ne wesan thu kwethan he Maria wreth 
319 thiorna thin siu wesan thihan wif 
320 ne farhuggian thu siu te hard thu skulan siu haldan wel 
321 wardon siu an these werold lestian thu inka winitreuwa 
322 forth so thu don endi haldan inka friundskepi wel 
323 ne latan thu siu thu the leth thoh siu undar iru lith egan 
324 barn an iru bosom it kuman thurh gibod god 
325 helag gest fan hevanwang 
326 the wesan Jesus Krist god egan barn 
327 waldand sunu thu skulan siu wel haldan 
328 helagliko ne latan thu thu thin hugi twiflian 
329 merrian thin modgithaht tho werthan eft the man hugi 
330 wendian aftar the word that he he te the wif niman 
331 te the magath minnia andkennian maht god 
332 waldand gibod wesan he willio mikil 
333 that he siu so helagliko haldan motan 
334 bisorgon siu an is gisith endi siu so suvro dragan 
335 al te huldi god helag gest 
336 godlik gumo untat siu god giskap 
337 mahtig manon that siu an man lioht 
338 al barn bet brengian skulan 
339 tho werthan fan Rumuburg riki man 
340 ovar al these irminthiod Octavian 
341 ban endi bodskepi ovar the is bred giwald 
342 kuman fan the kesur kuning gihwilik 
343 hemsittiand so wido so is heritogo 
344 ovar al the landskepi liudi waldan 
345 hetan man that al the elilendi man iru othil sokian 
346 helith iru handmahal angegin iru herro bodo 
347 kuman te the knosal gihwe thanan he kunni wesan 
348 beran fan the burg the gibod werthan lestian 
349 ovar these wid werold werod samnon 
350 to al burg gihwe faran the bodo ovar al 
351 the fan the kesur kuman wesan 
352 bokspahi wer an bref skrivan 
353 switho niudliko namo gihwilik 
354 ja land ja liudi that he ne mugan alettian man 
355 gumo sulik gambra so he skulan geldan gihwe 
356 helith fan is hovid tho witan he ok mid is hiwiski 
357 Joseph the god so it god mahtig 
358 waldand willian sokian he the wanam hem 
359 the burg an Bethlehem thar iru bethia wesan 
360 the helith handmahal endi ok the helag thiorna 
361 Maria the god thar wesan the mari stol 
362 an erdagos athalkunig 
363 David the god than lang the he the druhtskepi thar 
364 erl undar Ebreo egan motan 
365 haldan hohgiset he wesan is hiwiski 
366 kuman fan is knosal kunni god 
367 bethia bi giburd thar fregnan ik that siu the berht giskap 
368 Maria manon endi maht god 
369 that siu an the sith sunu odan werthan 
370 beran an Bethlehem barn strang 
371 al kuning kraftag kuman werthan the mari 
372 mahtig an man lioht so it er manag dag 
373 bilithi wesan endi bokan filo 
374 werthan an these werold tho wesan it al waron so 
375 so it er spahi man sprekan hebbian 
376 thurh hwilik othmodi he these erthriki herod 
377 thurh he self kraft sokian willian 
378 manag mundboro tho he the modar niman 
379 biwindan he mid uuad wif skoni 
380 fagar frataha endi he mid iru folm twene 
381 leggian liofliko luttil man 
382 the kind an en kribbia thoh he hebbian kraft god 
383 man drohtin thar sittian the modar biforan 
384 wif wakon wardon self 
385 haldan the helag barn ne wesan siu hugi twifli 
386 the magath iru modsevo tho werthan manag kuth 
387 ovar these wid werold ward andfindan 
388 the thar ehuskalk uta wesan 
389 wer an wahta wig gomian 
390 fehu aftar feld sehan finistri an twene 
391 telatan an luft endi kuman lioht god 
392 wanam thurh the wolkan endi the ward thar 
393 bifahan an the feld he werthan an forhta tho 
394 the man an iru mod sehan thar mahtig 
395 god engil kuman the he tegegnes sprekan 
396 hetan that he the ward wiht ne andradan 
397 leth fan the lioht ik skulan gi kwethan he liof thing 
398 switho warliko willio seggian 
399 kuthian kraft mikil nu wesan Krist beran 
400 an these self naht salig barn god 
401 an these David burg drohtin the god 
402 the wesan mendislo man kunni 
403 al firihos fruma thar gi he findan mugan 
404 an Bethlehemburg barn riki 
405 hebbian the te tekan that ik gi tellian mugan 
406 war word that he thar biwindan liggian 
407 the kind an en kribbia thoh he wesan kuning ovar al 
408 ertha endi himil endi ovar eldibarn 
409 werold waldand reht so he tho the word sprekan 
410 so werthan thar engil te the en unrim kuman 
411 helag heriskepi fan hevanwang 
412 fagar folk god endi filo sprekan 
413 lofword manag liudi herro 
414 afhebbian tho helag sang tho he eft te hevanwang 
415 windan thurh the wolkan the ward horian 
416 hwo the engil kraft alomahtig god 
417 switho warliko word lovon 
418 diuritha wesan nu kwethan he drohtin self 
419 an the hoh himil riki 
420 endi frithu an ertha firihos barn 
421 godwillig gumo the the god andkennian 
422 thurh hluttar hugi the hirdi farstandan 
423 that he mahtig thing manon hebbian 
424 blithi gibodskepi witan he te Bethlehem thanan 
425 naht sithon wesan he niud mikil 
426 that he self Krist sehan motan 
427 hebbian he the engil god al wisian 
428 torht tekan that he to he self 
429 to the god barn gangan mugan 
430 endi findan san folk drohtin 
431 liudi herro seggian tho lof god 
432 waldand mid iru word endi wido kuthian 
433 ovar the berht burg hwilik he thar bilithi werthan 
434 fan hevanwang helag togian 
435 fagar an feld the fri al bihaldan 
436 an iru hugiskaft helag thiorna 
437 the magath an iru mod so hwe so siu horian the man sprekan 
438 fodian he tho fagaro fri skoni 
439 the modar thurh minnia manag drohtin 
440 helag himilisk barn helith sprekan 
441 an the ahtodo dag erl manag 
442 switho glau gumo mid the god thiorna 
443 that he helian te namo hebbian skulan 
444 so it the god engil Gabriel sprekan 
445 war word endi the wif biodan 
446 bodo drohtin tho siu erist the barn andfahan 
447 wanam te these werold wesan siu willio mikil 
448 that siu he so helagliko haldan motan 
449 fulgangan he tho so gern the ger furthor skridan 
450 untat the frithubarn god fiuwartig hebbian 
451 dag endi naht tho skulan he thar en dad frummian 
452 that he he te Hierusalem fargevan skulan 
453 waldand te the wih tho wesan iru wisa than 
454 the liudi landsidu that the ne motan farlatan 
455 idis undar Ebreo ef siu odan werthan 
456 sunu afodian siu he simbla tharod 
457 te the god wih fargevan skulan 
458 witan he tho the god twene Joseph endi Maria 
459 bethia fan Bethlehem hebbian the barn mid he 
460 helag Krist sokian he hus god 
461 an Hierusalem thar skulan he is geld frummian 
462 waldand an the wih wisa lestian 
463 Judeo folk thar findan he en god man 
464 ald an the alah athalboran 
465 the hebbian an the wih so filo wintar endi sumar 
466 libbian an the lioht oft wirkian he thar lof god 
467 mid hluttar hugi hebbian he helag gest 
468 salig sevo Simeon wesan he hetan 
469 he hebbian wisian waldand kraft 
470 lang hwila that he ne motan er these lioht agevan 
471 wendian af these werold er than he the willio standan 
472 that he self Krist sehan motan 
473 helag hevankuning tho werthan he is hugi switho 
474 blithi an is briost tho he sehan the barn god kuman 
475 an the wih innan tho seggian he waldand thank 
476 alomahtig god the he he mid is oga sehan 
477 gangan he tho tegegnes endi he gern andfahan 
478 ald mid is arm al andkennian 
479 bokan endi bilithi endi ok the barn god 
480 helag hevankuning nu ik thu her skulan kwethan he 
481 gern biddian nu ik sus gamalon wesan 
482 that thu thin hold skalk nu hinan hwervan latan 
483 an thin frithu war faran thar er min forthero don 
484 wer fan these werold nu ik the willio standan 
485 dag liof that ik min drohtin sehan 
486 hold herro so ik hetan wesan 
487 lang hwila thu wesan lioht mikil 
488 al elithioda the er the alowaldo 
489 kraft ne andkennian thin kumi wesan 
490 te dom endi te diuritha drohtin fro min 
491 avaro Israhel egan folk 
492 thin liof liudi list tellian tho 
493 the ald man an the alah idis the god 
494 seggian sothlik hwo iru sunu skulan 
495 ovar these middilgard manag werthan 
496 sum te fal sum te frovra firihos barn 
497 the liudi te liof the is lera horian 
498 endi the te harm the horian ne willian 
499 Krist lera thu skulan noh kwethan he kara thiggian 
500 harm an thin herta than he helith barn 
501 wapan witnon the werthan thu werk mikil 
502 thrim te tholon the thiorna al farstandan 
503 wis man word tho kuman thar ok en wif gangan 
504 ald innan the alah Anna wesan siu hetan 
505 dohtar Fanuel siu hebbian iru drohtin wel 
506 thionon te thank wesan siu thihan wif 
507 siu motan aftar iru magathhed sithor siu man werthan 
508 erl an eht ethili thiorna 
509 so motan siu mid iru brudigumo bodal waldan 
510 sivun wintar saman tho fregnan ik that siu thar sorga standan 
511 that siu the mikil maht metod tedelian 
512 wreth wurdigiskap tho wesan siu widowa aftar the 
513 at the frithuwih fiuwar endi ahto 
514 wintar an iru werold so siu the wih ne farlatan 
515 ak siu thar iru drohtin dag endi naht 
516 god thionon siu kuman thar ok gangan to 
517 an the self tid san andkennian 
518 the helag barn god endi the helith kuthian 
519 the werod aftar the wih wilspel mikil 
520 kwethan that he nerian ginist nahian wesan 
521 helpa hevankuning nu wesan the helag Krist 
522 waldand self an these wih kuman 
523 to alosian the liudi the her nu lango bidan 
524 an these middilgard manag hwila 
525 thurftig thiod so nu the thing mugan 
526 mendian mankunni manag faganon 
527 werod aftar the wih horian wilspel mikil 
528 fan god seggian the geld hebbian tho lestian 
529 the idis an the alah al so it he an iru eo biodan 
530 endi an the berht burg bok wisian 
531 helag handgiwerk witan he tho te hus thanan 
532 fan Hierusalem Joseph endi Maria 
533 helag hiwiski hebbian he hevankuning 
534 simbla te gisith sunu drohtin 
535 manag mundboro so it eo mari ne werthan 
536 than wido an these werold newan so is willio gangan 
537 hevankuning hugi thoh thar than hwilik helag man 
538 Krist andkennian thoh ne werthan it eo te the kuning hof 
539 the man marian the he an iru modsevo 
540 hold ne wesan ak wesan he so bihaldan forth 
541 mid word endi mid werk untat thar wer ostan 
542 switho glau gumo gangan kuman 
543 thrie te the thiod thegan snel 
544 an lang weg ovar the land tharod 
545 folgon en berht bokan endi sokian the barn god 
546 mid hluttar hugi willian he hnigan to 
547 gehan he te jungaro drivan he god giskap 
548 tho he Erodes thar riki findan 
549 an is seli sittian slithwordi kuning 
550 modag mid is man simbla wesan he mod gern 
551 tho kweddian he he kusko an kuningwisa 
552 fagaro an is fletti endi he fragon san 
553 hwilik he arundi uta brengian 
554 wer an the wraksith hwethar ledian gi windan gold 
555 te geva hwilik gumo te hwe gi sus an gang kuman 
556 faran an fathi hwe gi nethwanan ferran wesan 
557 erl fan othar thiod ik sehan that gi wesan ethiligiburd 
558 kunni fan knosal god her er sulik kuman ne werthan 
559 er fan othar thiod sithor ik motan these erl folk 
560 waldan these wid riki gi skulan ik te war seggian 
561 for these liudi folk bihwi gi wesan te these land kuman 
562 tho sprekan he eft tegegnes gumo ostroni 
563 wordspah wer we thu te war mugan kwethan he 
564 usa arundi otho tellian 
565 seggian sothlik bihwi we kuman an these sith herod 
566 fan ostan te these ertha ju wesan thar athali man 
567 godspraki gumo the we god so filo 
568 helpa hetan fan hevankuning 
569 war word than wesan thar en giwittig man 
570 frod endi filowis forn wesan the ju 
571 usa aldiro ostar hinan thar ne werthan sithor enig man 
572 spraka so spah he mugan rekkian spel god

577 agevan gard gaduling gimang

582 werthan an these werold tho seggian he that her skulan kuman en wiskuning 
583 mari endi mahtig an these middilgard

585 kwethan that he these werold waldan skulan

2700 lerian the liudi langsam rad

2704 the heritogo at hus the hetan wesan 
2705 Erodes aftar is eldiro ovarmodig man 
2706 buan he bi the brud the er sin brothar wesan 
2707 idis an eht untat he ellior skakan 
2708 werold wehslon tho he the wif niman 
2709 the kuning te kwen er wesan siu kind odan 
2710 barn bi is brothar tho biginnan he the brud lahan 
2711 Johannes the god kwethan that it god wesan 
2712 waldand witharmod that it enig wer frummian 
2713 that brothar brud an is bed niman 
2714 hebbian siu he te hiwa ef thu ik horian willian 
2715 lovian min lera ne skulan thu siu lango egan 
2716 ak mithan siu an thin mod ne hebbian thu thar sulik minnia to 
2717 ne sundion thu te switho tho werthan an sorga hugi 
2718 the wif aftar the word andradan that he the weroldkuning 
2719 spraka spanan endi spah word 
2720 that he siu farlatan biginnan siu he tho leth filo 
2721 radan an runa endi he rink hetan 
2722 unsundig erl fahan

2724 lithokosp bilucan bi the liudi ne durran

2739 wesan an wunnia dragan man win an flet

2748 grotian siu for the gumskepi endi gern biddian

2750 fagar an fletti latan these folk sehan

2754 liohto for these liudi endi ok lestian so

2756 so hwe so thu ik biddian for these min bogwini

2758 riki min thoh don ik that it enig rink ne mugan

2765 hror aftar the hus hugi wesan an lust

4015 serag sittian wesan thar samnon filo 
4016 fan Hierusalem Judeo liudi 
4017 the the wif willian word frovrian 
4018 that siu so ne karon kindjung doth 
4019 Lazarus farlust so tho the land ward 
4020 gangan an the gard so werthan the god barn 
4021 kumi thar kwethan that he so kraftag wesan 
4022 bi the burg utan tho siu bethia wesan 
4023 the wif sulik willio that siu siu waldand Krist to 
4024 the frithubarn god faran witan 
4025 tho the wif wesan willio mer 
4026 kumi drohtin endi Krist word 
4027 te horian hiovan gangan 
4028 Martha modkarag with so mahtig 
4029 word wehslon endi with waldand sprekan 
4030 an iru hugi hriuwig thar thu ik herro min kwethan siu 
4031 nerian bet nah wesan 
4032 helian the god than ne thurvan ik nu sulik harm tholon 
4033 bittar briostkara than ne wesan nu min brothar dod 
4034 Lazarus fan these lioht ak he mugan he libbian forth 
4035 ferah fullian ik thoh fro min te thu 
4036 liohto lovian lerian bet 
4037 so hwe so thu biddian willian berht drohtin 
4038 that he it thu san fargevan god alomahtig 
4039 werthon thin willio tho sprekan eft waldand Krist 
4040 the idis andwordi ne latan thu thu an innan the kwethan he 
4041 thin sevo swerkan ik thu seggian mugan 
4042 war word that the giwand enig 
4043 thin brothar skulan thurh gibod god 
4044 thurh drohtin kraft fan doth astandan 
4045 an is likhamo al hebbian ik gilovo so kwethan siu 
4046 that it so werthan skulan so hwan so these werold endion 
4047 endi the mari dag ovar man faran 
4048 that he than fan ertha skulan up astandan 
4049 an the dom dag than werthan fan doth kwik 
4050 thurh maht god mankunni gihwilik 
4051 arisan fan rasta tho seggian riki Krist 
4052 the idis alomahtig opan word 
4053 that he self wesan sunu drohtin 
4054 bethia ge lioht ge lif liudi barn 
4055 te astandan the astervan ne skulan 
4056 lif farliosan the her lovian te ik 
4057 thoh he eldibarn ertha bithekkian 
4058 diopo bidelvan he dod the mer 
4059 the flesk wesan bifelhan the ferah wesan haldan 
4060 wesan the seola gisund tho sprekan he eft san angegin

4069 an iru hugi harm hofna kumian 
4070 Lazarus farlust liof man 
4071 gratan gornon untat the god barn 
4072 hugi werthan hrorian het trahn 
4073 wop awellan endi tho te the wif sprekan 
4074 hetan he tho ledian thar Lazarus wesan 
4075 folda bifelhan liggian thar en felis biovan 
4076 hard sten bihlidan tho hetan the helag Krist 
4077 andlukan the hleo that he motan the lik sehan 
4078 hreo skauwon tho ne mugan an iru hugi mithan 
4079 Martha for the menigi with mahtig sprekan 
4080 fro min the god kwethan siu ef man the felis niman 
4081 the sten andlukan than wanian ik that thanan stank kuman 
4082 unswoti swek hwand ik thu seggian mugan 
4083 war word that the giwand enig

5766 wer an the wahta wanam naht 
5767 bidan undar he bord hwan er the berht dag 
5768 ovar middilgard man kuman 
5769 liudi te lioht tho ne wesan lang te the 
5770 that thar werthan the gest kuman bi god kraft 
5771 helag athom undar the hard sten 
5772 an the likhamo lioht wesan tho opanon 
5773 firihos barn te fruma wesan ferkal manag 
5774 andheftian fan heldor endi te himil wag 
5775 wirkian fan these werold wanam up astandan 
5776 frithubarn god faran he tho thar he willian 
5777 so the ward the wiht ne afsebbian 
5778 dervi liudi hwan he fan the doth astandan 
5779 arisan fan the rasta rink sittian 
5780 umbi the graf utan Judeo liudi 
5781 skola mid he skild skridan forthward 
5782 swigli sunno lioht sithon idis 
5783 te the graf gangan gumkunni wif 
5784 Maria munilik hebbian methom filo 
5785 sellian withar salva siluvar endi gold 
5786 werth withar wurt so siu mugan awinnan mer 
5787 that siu the likhamo liof herro 
5788 sunu drohtin salvon motan 
5789 wunda writan the wif sorgon 
5790 an siu sevo switho endi sum sprekan 
5791 hwe siu the grot sten fan the graf skulan 
5792 hwervian an halva the siu ovar the hreo sehan 
5793 the liudi leggian tho he the likhamo thar 
5794 bifelhan an the felis so the fri hebbian 
5795 gangan te the gardo that siu te the graf mugan 
5796 sehan self tho thar swogan kuman 
5797 engil the alowaldo ovana fan radur 
5798 faran an fetherhamo that al the folda anskannan 
5799 the ertha dunnian endi the erl werthan 
5800 an wek hugi ward Judeo 
5801 bifallan bi the forhta ne wanian he ferah egan 
5802 lif lang hwila liggian than ward 
5803 the gisith samkwik san up ahlidan 
5804 the grot sten fan the graf so he the god engil 
5805 hwervian an halva endi he uppan the hleo sittian 
5806 diurlik drohtin bodo he wesan an he dad gilik 
5807 an he ansiuni so hwe so he motan undar he oga skauwon 
5808 so berht endi so blithi al so bliksmo lioht 
5809 wesan he he giwadi wintarkald 
5810 sneo gilik tho sehan he he sittian thar 
5811 the wif uppan the wendian sten endi siu fan the wliti standan 
5812 the idis sulik egiso tegegnes al werthan 
5813 the fri an forhta fan the gruri mikil furthor ne durran 
5814 te the graf gangan er siu the god engil 
5815 waldand bodo word grotian 
5816 kwethan that he siu arundi al bikunnan 
5817 werk endi willio endi the wif hugi 
5818 hetan that siu he ne andradan ik witan that gi iuwa drohtin sokian 
5819 nerian Krist fan Nazarethburg 
5820 the the her kwellian endi an kruci slahan 
5821 Judeo liudi endi an graf leggian 
5822 sundilos nu he self her 
5823 ak he wesan astandan ju endi wesan these stedi lari 
5824 these graf an these griot nu mugan gi gangan herod 
5825 nah mikil ik witan that he gi wesan niud sehan 
5826 an these sten innan her wesan noh the stedi skin 
5827 thar he likhamo liggian lungar fahan 
5828 gibada an siu briost blek idis 
5829 wlitiskoni wif wesan siu wilspel mikil 
5830 te horian the siu fan siu herro seggian 
5831 engil the alowaldo hetan siu eft thanan 
5832 fan the graf gangan endi faran te the jungaro Krist 
5833 seggian the he gisith soth word 
5834 that he drohtin wesan fan doth astandan 
5835 hetan ok an sundar Simon Petrus 
5836 wilspel mikil word kuthian 
5837 kumi drohtin ge that Krist self 
5838 wesan an Galilea land thar he eft he jungaro skulan 
5839 sehan he gisith so he he er self sprekan 
5840 war word reht so tho the wif thanan 
5841 gangan willian so standan siu tegegnes thar 
5842 engil twene an alahwit 
5843 wanam giwadi endi sprekan siu mid he word to 
5844 helagliko hugi werthan blothian 
5845 the idis an egiso ne mugan an the engil god 
5846 bi the wliti skauwon wesan siu the wanami te strang 
5847 te swith te sehan tho sprekan siu san angegin 
5848 waldand bodo endi the wif fragon 
5849 te hwe siu Krist tharod kwik mid dod 
5850 sunu drohtin sokian kuman 
5851 ferah ful nu gi he ne findan her 
5852 an these stengraf ak he wesan astandan nu 
5853 an he likhamo the gi lovian skulan 
5854 endi huggian the word the he gi te war oft 
5855 self seggian than he an iuwa gisithi wesan 
5856 an Galilealand hwo he skulan gevan werthan 
5857 sellian self an sundig man 
5858 hettian hand helag drohtin 
5859 that he he kwellian endi an kruci slahan 
5860 dod don endi that he skulan thurh drohtin kraft 
5861 an thriddio dag thiod te willio 
5862 libbian astandan nu hebbian he al lestian so 
5863 frummian mid firihos ilian gi nu forth hinan 
5864 gangan gahliko endi don it the he jungaro kuth 
5865 he hebbian siu ju furfaran endi wesan he forth hinan 
5866 an Galilea land thar he eft he jungaro skulan 
5867 sehan he gisith tho werthan san aftar the 
5868 the wif an willio that siu horian sulik word sprekan 
5869 kuthian the kraft god wesan siu so akuman tho noh 
5870 ge so forht frummian witan siu forth thanan 
5871 fan the graf gangan endi seggian the jungaro Krist 
5872 seldlik gisiun thar siu sorgon 
5873 bidan sulik bota tho werthan ok an the burg kuman 
5874 Judeo ward the ovar the graf sittian 
5875 al lang naht endi the likhamo thar 
5876 hodian the hreo he seggian the heri Judeo 
5877 hwilik siu thar andward egiso kuman 
5878 seldlik gisiun seggian mid word 
5879 al so it don wesan an the drohtin kraft 
5880 ne mithan an he mod tho biodan he methom filo 
5881 Judeo liudi gold endi siluvar 
5882 sellian he sink manag te the that he it ne seggian forth 
5883 marian the menigi ak kwethan that gi mothi hugi 
5884 answebbian mid slap endi that thar kuman gisith to 
5885 farstelan he an the sten simnon wesan gi an strid mid the 
5886 forth an flit ef it werthan the folktogo kuth 
5887 we helpan gi with the her that he gi harm wiht 
5888 leth ne lestian tho niman he an the liudi filo 
5889 diuri methom don al so he biginnan 
5890 ne waldan he willio kuth 
5891 the liudi aftar the land that he sulik lugina willian 
5892 ahebbian bi the helag drohtin than wesan eft helian hugi 
5893 jungaro Krist tho he horian the god wif 
5894 marian the maht god tho wesan he an he mod fra 
5895 ge he te the graf bethia Johannes endi Petrus 
5896 rinnan ovastliko werthan er kuman 
5897 Johannes the god endi he ovar the graf standan 
5898 untat thar san aftar kuman Simon Petrus 
5899 erl ellianrof endi he thar in witan 
5900 an the graf gangan sehan thar the god barn 
5901 hreogiwadi herro sin 
5902 linin liggian mid the wesan er the likhamo 
5903 fagaro bifahan liggian the fano sundar 
5904 mid the wesan the hovid bihellian helag Krist 
5905 riki drohtin than he an these rasta wesan 
5906 tho gangan he ok Johannes an the graf innan 
5907 sehan seldlik thing werthan he san aftar the 
5908 andlukan he gilovo that he witan that skulan eft an these lioht kuman 
5909 he drohtin diurliko fan doth astandan 
5910 up fan ertha tho witan he eft thanan 
5911 Johannes endi Petrus endi kuman the jungaro Krist 
5912 the gisith tesamna than standan seragmod 
5913 en the idis othar sith 
5914 griotan ovar the graf wesan siu jamar mod 
5915 Maria wesan the Magdalena wesan siu modgithaht 
5916 sevo mid sorga sero blandan ne witan hwarod siu sokian skulan 
5917 the herro thar siu wesan at the helpa gilang siu ne mugan tho hofna awisian 
5918 the wif ne mugan wop farlatan ne witan hwarod siu siu wendian skulan 
5919 merrian wesan siu the modgithaht tho sehan siu the mahtig thar standan 
5920 Krist thoh siu he kuthliko andkennian ne mugan er than he he kuthian willian 
5921 seggian that he it self wesan he fragon hwe siu so sero biwopian 
5922 so harm mid het trahn siu kwethan that siu umbi siu herro ne witan 
5923 te war hwarod he werthan skulan ef thu he ik wisian mugan 
5924 fro min ef ik thu fragon durran ef thu he her an these felis niman 
5925 wisian he ik mid word thin than wesan ik al willio mer 
5926 that ik he self sehan siu ne witan that siu the sunu drohtin 
5927 grotian mid god spraka siu wanian that it the gardari wesan 
5928 hofward herro sin tho grotian siu the helag drohtin 
5929 bi namo nerian bet siu gangan he tho nah sniumo 
5930 the wif mid willio god andkennian siu waldand self 
5931 mithan siu he thurh the minnia ne witan willian he mid siu mund gripan 
5932 the femia an the folk drohtin newan that siu frithubarn god 
5933 werian mid word sin kwethan that siu he mid wiht ne motan 
5934 hand andhrinan ik ne stigan noh kwethan he te the himilisk fadar 
5935 ak ilian thu nu ovastliko endi the erl kuthian 
5936 brothar min that ik usa bethia fadar 
5937 alowaldo iuwa endi min 
5938 sothfast god sokian willian 
5939 the wif werthan tho an wunnia that siu motan sulik willio kuthian 
5940 seggian fan he gisund werthan san garu 
5941 the idis an the arundi endi the erl brengian 
5942 wilspel wer that siu waldand Krist 
5943 gisund sehan endi seggian hwo he siu self biodan 
5944 torht tekan he ne willian truon tho noh 
5945 the wif word that siu sulik wilspel brengian 
5946 gegnungo fan the god sunu ak he sittian he jamarmod 
5947 helith hriuwon tho werthan the helag Krist 
5948 eft opanliko othar sith 
5949 drohtin togian sithor he fan doth astandan 
5950 the wif an willio that he he thar an weg motian 
5951 kweddian he kuthliko endi he te he knio hnigan 
5952 fallan he to fot he hetan that he forht hugi 
5953 ne beran an he briost ak gi min brothar skulan 
5954 these kwidi kuthian that he kuman aftar ik 
5955 an Galilea land thar ik he eft tegegnes wesan 
5956 than faran he ok fan Hierusalem the jungaro twene 
5957 an the self dag san an morgan 
5958 erl an he arundi willian he te Emaus 
5959 the kastel sokian tho biginnan he kwidi manag 
5960 undar the wer wahsan thar he aftar the weg faran 
5961 the helith umbi he herro tho kuman he thar the helag to 
5962 gangan god sunu he ne mugan he garoliko 
5963 andkennian kraftag he ne willian he tho noh kuthian te he 
5964 wesan he thoh an he gisithi samad endi fragon umbi hwilik he saka sprekan 
5965 hwe gangan gi so gornon kwethan he wesan gi jamar hugi 
5966 sevo sorga ful he sprekan he san angegin 
5967 the erl andwordi te hwe thu the so eskon kwethan he 
5968 wesan thu fan Hierusalem Judeo folk
